  <script type="text/javascript">
    (function() {
        var contextPath = '/jira';
        var eventBuffer = [];

        function printDeprecatedMsg() {
            if (console && console.warn) {
                console.warn('DEPRECATED JS - contextPath global variable has been deprecated since 7.4.0. Use `wrm/context-path` module instead.');
            }
        }

        function sendEvent(analytics, postfix) {
            analytics.send({
                name: 'js.globals.contextPath.' + postfix
            });
        }

        function sendDeprecatedEvent(postfix) {
            try {
                var analytics = require('jira/analytics');
                if (eventBuffer.length) {
                    eventBuffer.forEach(function(value) {
                        sendEvent(analytics, value);
                    });
                    eventBuffer = [];
                }

                if (postfix) {
                    sendEvent(analytics, postfix);
                }
            } catch(ex) {
                eventBuffer.push(postfix);
                setTimeout(sendDeprecatedEvent, 1000);
            }
        }

        Object.defineProperty(window, 'contextPath', {
            get: function() {
                printDeprecatedMsg();
                sendDeprecatedEvent('get');
                return contextPath;
            },
            set: function(value) {
                printDeprecatedMsg();
                sendDeprecatedEvent('set');
                contextPath = value;
            }
        });
    })();

</script>

              <div id="descriptionmodule" class="module toggle-wrap">
               <div id="descriptionmodule_heading" class="mod-header">
                <ul class="ops"></ul>
                <h2 class="toggle-title">Description</h2>
               </div>
               <div class="mod-content">
                <div id="description-val" class="field-ignore-highlight"> 
                 <div class="user-content-block"> 
                  <p>Our setup is based on multiple cores. In One core we have a multi-filed with integer values. and some other unimportant fields. We're using multi-faceting for this field.</p> 
                  <p>We're querying a test scenario with:</p> 
                  <div class="code panel" style="border-width: 1px;">
                   <div class="codeContent panelContent"> 
                    <pre class="code-java">http:<span class="code-comment">//localhost:8983/solr/core-name/select?q=dummyask: (<span class="code-keyword">true</span>) AND manufacturer: <span class="code-keyword">false</span> AND id: (15039 16882 10850 20781)&amp;fq={!tag=professions}professions: (59)&amp;fl=id&amp;wt=json&amp;indent=<span class="code-keyword">true</span>&amp;facet=<span class="code-keyword">true</span>&amp;facet.field={!ex=professions}professions</span>
</pre> 
                   </div>
                  </div> 
                  <ul class="alternate" type="square"> 
                   <li>Query: (numDocs:48545, maxDoc:48545) 
                    <div class="code panel" style="border-width: 1px;">
                     <div class="codeContent panelContent"> 
                      <pre class="code-xml"><span class="code-tag">&lt;response&gt;</span>
<span class="code-tag">&lt;lst name=<span class="code-quote">"responseHeader"</span>&gt;</span>
<span class="code-tag">&lt;int name=<span class="code-quote">"status"</span>&gt;</span>0<span class="code-tag">&lt;/int&gt;</span>
<span class="code-tag">&lt;int name=<span class="code-quote">"QTime"</span>&gt;</span>1<span class="code-tag">&lt;/int&gt;</span>
<span class="code-tag">&lt;/lst&gt;</span>
<span class="code-tag">&lt;result name=<span class="code-quote">"response"</span> numFound=<span class="code-quote">"4"</span> start=<span class="code-quote">"0"</span>&gt;</span>
<span class="code-tag">&lt;doc&gt;</span>
<span class="code-tag">&lt;int name=<span class="code-quote">"id"</span>&gt;</span>10850<span class="code-tag">&lt;/int&gt;</span>
<span class="code-tag">&lt;/doc&gt;</span>
<span class="code-tag">&lt;doc&gt;</span>
<span class="code-tag">&lt;int name=<span class="code-quote">"id"</span>&gt;</span>16882<span class="code-tag">&lt;/int&gt;</span>
<span class="code-tag">&lt;/doc&gt;</span>
<span class="code-tag">&lt;doc&gt;</span>
<span class="code-tag">&lt;int name=<span class="code-quote">"id"</span>&gt;</span>15039<span class="code-tag">&lt;/int&gt;</span>
<span class="code-tag">&lt;/doc&gt;</span>
<span class="code-tag">&lt;doc&gt;</span>
<span class="code-tag">&lt;int name=<span class="code-quote">"id"</span>&gt;</span>20781<span class="code-tag">&lt;/int&gt;</span>
<span class="code-tag">&lt;/doc&gt;</span>
<span class="code-tag">&lt;/result&gt;</span>
<span class="code-tag">&lt;lst name=<span class="code-quote">"facet_counts"</span>&gt;</span>
<span class="code-tag">&lt;lst name=<span class="code-quote">"facet_queries"</span>/&gt;</span>
<span class="code-tag">&lt;lst name=<span class="code-quote">"facet_fields"</span>&gt;</span>
<span class="code-tag">&lt;lst name=<span class="code-quote">"professions"</span>&gt;</span>
<span class="code-tag">&lt;int name=<span class="code-quote">"59"</span>&gt;</span>4<span class="code-tag">&lt;/int&gt;</span>
<span class="code-tag">&lt;/lst&gt;</span>
<span class="code-tag">&lt;/lst&gt;</span>
<span class="code-tag">&lt;lst name=<span class="code-quote">"facet_dates"</span>/&gt;</span>
<span class="code-tag">&lt;lst name=<span class="code-quote">"facet_ranges"</span>/&gt;</span>
<span class="code-tag">&lt;lst name=<span class="code-quote">"facet_intervals"</span>/&gt;</span>
<span class="code-tag">&lt;lst name=<span class="code-quote">"facet_heatmaps"</span>/&gt;</span>
<span class="code-tag">&lt;/lst&gt;</span>
<span class="code-tag">&lt;/response&gt;</span>
</pre> 
                     </div>
                    </div></li> 
                   <li>Then we update one document and change some fields (numDocs:48545, maxDoc:48546) <b>The number of maxDocs is increased</b> 
                    <div class="code panel" style="border-width: 1px;">
                     <div class="codeContent panelContent"> 
                      <pre class="code-xml"><span class="code-tag">&lt;response&gt;</span>
<span class="code-tag">&lt;lst name=<span class="code-quote">"responseHeader"</span>&gt;</span>
<span class="code-tag">&lt;int name=<span class="code-quote">"status"</span>&gt;</span>0<span class="code-tag">&lt;/int&gt;</span>
<span class="code-tag">&lt;int name=<span class="code-quote">"QTime"</span>&gt;</span>1<span class="code-tag">&lt;/int&gt;</span>
<span class="code-tag">&lt;/lst&gt;</span>
<span class="code-tag">&lt;result name=<span class="code-quote">"response"</span> numFound=<span class="code-quote">"4"</span> start=<span class="code-quote">"0"</span>&gt;</span>

<span class="code-tag">&lt;/doc&gt;</span>
<span class="code-tag">&lt;doc&gt;</span>
<span class="code-tag">&lt;int name=<span class="code-quote">"id"</span>&gt;</span>16882<span class="code-tag">&lt;/int&gt;</span>
<span class="code-tag">&lt;/doc&gt;</span>
<span class="code-tag">&lt;doc&gt;</span>

<span class="code-tag">&lt;/doc&gt;</span>
<span class="code-tag">&lt;/result&gt;</span>
<span class="code-tag">&lt;lst name=<span class="code-quote">"facet_counts"</span>&gt;</span>
<span class="code-tag">&lt;lst name=<span class="code-quote">"facet_queries"</span>/&gt;</span>
<span class="code-tag">&lt;lst name=<span class="code-quote">"facet_fields"</span>&gt;</span>

                     </div>
                    </div></li> 
                  </ul> 
                  <p><b>The Problem:</b><br> In the first query, we're getting a facet count of 4, which is correct. After updating one document, we're getting 5 as a result wich is not correct.</p>

Since all the documents in the core have unique values for all fields, all facet queries should give count \u003ctt\u003e1\u003c\\/tt\u003e for all values for all fields. Simple facet queries return correct results:\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003equery is \u003ctt\u003eq=&#42;:&#42;&amp;rows=0&amp;facet=true&amp;facet.limit=1&amp;facet.field=foo_s&amp;facet.field=foo_i&amp;facet.field=bar_s&amp;facet.field=bar_i\u003c\\/tt\u003e\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\nresponse \\\"facet_fields\\\":{\\n      \\\"foo_s\\\":[\\\"1\\\",1],\\n      \\\"foo_i\\\":[\\\"1\\\",1],\\n      \\\"bar_s\\\":[\\\"1\\\",1],\\n      \\\"bar_i\\\":[\\\"1\\\",1]\\n    },\\n    \\\"facet_dates\\\":{},\\n    \\\"facet_ranges\\\":{},\\n    \\\"facet_intervals\\\":{},\\n is I selected the following parameters: \\n \\n\\t Request-Handler (qt):  \\/update\\/json ; \\n\\t Document Type:  Solr Command (raw XML or JSON) ; \\n\\t Documents set to the above JSON generate in python interpreter. \\n \\n\\n\\n After the Solr core is filled with documents, I add a single document once again, so this document overwrites the previous one: \\n  \\n {\'bar_s\': 2, \'foo_i\': 2, \'bar_i\': 2, \'foo_s\': 2, \'id\': 2}\\n \\n  \\n\\n Now when I look at the \\\"Overview\\\" tab I see the following statistics: \\n  \\n Last Modified: less than a minute ago\\nNum Docs: 20\\nMax Doc: 21\\nHeap Memory Usage: -1\\nDeleted Docs: 1\\nVersion: 7\\nSegment Count: 2\\n \\n  \\n\\n And at this stage all multi select facet queries give incorrect results. Since all the documents in the core have unique values for all fields, all facet queries should give count  1  for all values for all fields. Simple facet queries return correct results: \\n\\n query is  q=&#42;:&#42;&amp;rows=0&amp;facet=true&amp;facet.limit=1&amp;facet.field=foo_s&amp;facet.field=foo_i&amp;facet.field=bar_s&amp;facet.field=bar_i  \\nresponse is \\n  \\n {\\n  \\\"responseHeader\\\":{\\\"status\\\":0,\\\"QTime\\\":1},\\n  \\\"response\\\":{\\\"numFound\\\":20,\\\"start\\\":0,\\\"docs\\\":[]},\\n  \\\"facet_counts\\\":{\\n    \\\"facet_queries\\\":{},\\n    \\\"facet_fields\\\":{\\n      \\\"foo_s\\\":[\\\"1\\\",1],\\n      \\\"foo_i\\\":[\\\"1\\\",1],\\n      \\\"bar_s\\\":[\\\"1\\\",1],\\n      \\\"bar_i\\\":[\\\"1\\\",1]\\n    },\\n    \\\"facet_dates\\\":{},\\n    \\\"facet_ranges\\\":{},\\n    \\\"facet_intervals\\\":{},\\n    \\\"facet_heatmaps\\\":{}}}\\n \\n  \\n\\n And this is what we get for multi select facet query: \\n\\n query is  q=&#42;:&#42;&amp;fq={!tag=a}id:&#42;&amp;rows=0&amp;facet=true&amp;facet.limit=1&amp;facet.field={!ex=a}foo_s&amp;facet.field={!ex=a}foo_i&amp;facet.field={!ex=a}bar_s&amp;facet.field={!ex=a}bar_i  \\nresponse is \\n  \\n {\\n  \\\"responseHeader\\\":{\\\"status\\\":0,\\\"QTime\\\":2},\\n  \\\"response\\\":{\\\"numFound\\\":20,\\\"start\\\":0,\\\"docs\\\":[]},\\n  \\\"facet_counts\\\":{\\n    \\\"facet_queries\\\":{},\\n    \\\"facet_fields\\\":{\\n      \\\"foo_s\\\":[\\\"2\\\",2],\\n      \\\"foo_i\\\":[\\\"2\\\",2],\\n      \\\"bar_s\\\":[\\\"2\\\",2],\\n      \\\"bar_i\\\":[\\\"2\\\",2]},\\n    \\\"facet_dates\\\":{},\\n    \\\"facet_ranges\\\":{},\\n    \\\"facet_intervals\\\":{},\\n    \\\"facet_heatmaps\\\":{}}}\\n \\n  \\n\\n So we get count  2  for value  \\\"2\\\" , i.e. replaced (old) version of the document with  id=2  is taken into account when using multi selection facets.              \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n        \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n
